## Objective
- `intended_outcome`: Close the frontmatter migration cycle by replacing the custom YAML subset parser with a supported library, preserving the entity-document contract, and adding regression coverage for risky round-trip cases.
- `scope_boundary`: Limited to the frontmatter migration story, its Flywheel state transitions, the observer artifact, and cleanup of accidentally tracked `Source/node_modules`; no broader product work or RBAC follow-up changes were included.

## Inputs And Evidence
- `artifacts_reviewed`: AGENTS.md; Flywheel/flywheel.yaml; Flywheel prompts and role contracts; STORY-20260415-worldforge-frontmatter-yaml-library-migration.md; package metadata; automated validation output
- `tools_used`: apply_patch; exec_command; multi_tool_use.parallel; git; Flywheel observer script
- `external_sources`: none

## Changes Made
- `files_changed`: frontmatter parser and tests, package metadata, engineering queue artifacts, observer report, and git index cleanup for previously tracked Source/node_modules
- `state_transitions`: frontmatter migration story moved intake -> active -> qa -> done
- `non_file_actions`: untracked Source/node_modules from git while preserving the local install; reran typecheck, test, and build as QA evidence

- `checks_run`: `pnpm run typecheck`; `pnpm run test`; `pnpm run build`; focused `pnpm exec vitest run world/frontmatter.test.ts world/document.test.ts`
- `results`: all checks passed; QA confirmed acceptance criteria coverage and no blocking defects
- `checks_not_run`: no browser-driven manual editor save pass beyond automated round-trip and document-store coverage

- [x] Entry docs updated if workflow behavior changed.

- `assumptions_carried`: semantic round-trip safety matters more than preserving exact prior formatting quirks; unsupported rich YAML types remain out of scope for the entity-document contract
- `warnings`: this cycle intentionally removes a previously tracked dependency tree from git, so the resulting commit includes a large deletion set for Source/node_modules
